# Dyanstic/Monarch Events
namespace = vef_dynasty

# Chances of birth for all lower order members are calculated off their age (even though a
# male could hypothetically have a much younger or older wife).

#1 Monarch moves their crown if main union nation is badly beaten
#2 Iure Uxoris becomes a union on heir death without replacement and the other kingdom has heir
#3 Overlord Event (from dynasty.2)
#4 Iure Uxoris becomes a union if a new male heir is born to the overlord and the subject has no heir

#Heirs & Queens
#100 Aging Pulse, Death, & Generation
#101 Queen With Child
#102 Miscarriage
#103 Queen Dies in Childbirth - Child Survives
#104 Healthy Birth
#105 Queen Dies - Non-DLC
#106 Heir Dies
#107 Queen Dies in Childbirth - Child Dies
#108 Ruler With child
#109 Ruler Miscarries
#110 Ruler Dies in Childbirth - Child Survives
#111 Ruler Dies in Childbirth - Child Dies
#112 Heir Dies (On-Action)
#113 Ruler Dies (On-Action)
#114 Queen With Child - No DLC
#115 Miscarriage - No DLC

#Need For An Heir Events
#200 Married With No Children, Getting Old
#201 Older Ruler, Not Married, No Sons, Has Illegitimate Children

#Military Prowess
#300 - 304 Ruler +
#305 - 309 Heir +
#310 - 314 Ruler -
#315 - 319 Heir -


# Monarch moves his/her crown
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.1
	title = "vef_dynasty.1.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.1.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #on_actions/on_war_lost
	
	trigger = {
		personal_union = 1
		NOT = { total_development = 50 }
		NOT = { tag = MOS } #Keep Moscow from swapping with Vladimir-Suzdal
		NOT = { any_country = { war_with = ROOT }}
		any_subject_country = {
			junior_union_with = ROOT
			NOT = { is_subject_of_type = bohemian_union }
			num_of_cities = ROOT
			NOT = { ROOT = { num_of_cities = PREV }}
		}
		ai = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.1.opta"
		random_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				junior_union_with = ROOT
				NOT = { is_subject_of_type = bohemian_union }
				num_of_cities = ROOT
				NOT = { ROOT = { num_of_cities = PREV }}
			}
			hidden_effect = { transfer_royal_family = yes }
			ROOT = { hidden_effect = { exile_ruler_as = transfer_monarch_@ROOT }}
			overlord = { break_union = PREV }
			set_ruler = transfer_monarch_@ROOT
			create_union = ROOT
		}
	}
}

# Iure Uxoris becomes a union on heir death without replacement and the other kingdom has heir
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.2
	title = "vef_dynasty.2.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.2.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #on_actions/on_heir_death
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject_of_type = iure_uxoris
		has_heir = no
		overlord = { has_heir = yes }
	}

	option = {
		overlord = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.3 }}
	}
}

# Iure Uxoris becomes a union on heir death without replacement and the other kingdom has heir
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.3
	title = "vef_dynasty.3.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.3.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #vef_dynasty.2

	option = {
		FROM = { grant_independence = yes }
		create_union = FROM
	}
}

# Iure Uxoris senior has male heir without an heir in the junior (possible in some starts)
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.4
	title = "vef_dynasty.4.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.4.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #on_actions/on_new_heir

	trigger = {
		has_female_heir = no
		any_subject_country = {
			is_subject_of_type = iure_uxoris
			has_heir = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of_type = iure_uxoris
				has_heir = no
			}
			grant_independence = yes
			ROOT = { create_union = PREV }
		}
	}
}

#Aging Pulse and Maintenance Event
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.100
	title = "vef_dynasty.100.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.100.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture

	hidden = yes
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		NOT = { has_reform = iqta }
		NOT = { has_reform = mamluk_government }
		OR = {
			NOT = { tag = FRA }
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_tour_de_nesle }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_nesle_conviction }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		##CONCEPTION
		#RULER
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes } NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_pregnancy }}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" }
					NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
					NOT = { ruler_age = 50 }
					is_female = no
				#	check_variable = { which = queen_age value = 192 }
				#	NOT = { check_variable = { which = queen_age value = 600 }}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { ruler_age = 30 }
					#	NOT = { check_variable = { which = queen_age value = 360 }}
					}
					random = {
						chance = 4
						set_country_flag = vef_pregnancy
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage }}
							random_list = {
								24 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 35 }}
								1 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 35 }}
								24 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 42 }}
								1 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 42 }}

								1 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 49 }}

							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2 }
							random_list = {

								7 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 35 }}

								7 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 42 }}
								18 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 49 }}
								7 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 49 }}
								18 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 56 }}
								7 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 56 }}
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3 }
							random_list = {
								10 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 35 }}
								15 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 35 }}
								10 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 42 }}
								15 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 42 }}
								10 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 49 }}
								15 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 49 }}
								10 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 56 }}
								15 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 56 }}

						}
						else = {
							random_list = {

								3 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 35 }}
								22 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 42 }}
								3 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 42 }}
								22 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 49 }}
								3 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 49 }}
								22 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.114 days = 56 }}
								3 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.115 days = 56 }}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {

# Queen With Child
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.101
	title = "vef_dynasty.101.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.101.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = vef_pregnancy_known
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.101.opta"
	}
}

# Miscarriage
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.102
	title = "vef_dynasty.102.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.102.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = vef_pregnancy
		set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2 }
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1 }
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3 }}
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.102.opta"
	}
}

# Death in Childbirth - Child Survives
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.103
	title = "vef_dynasty.103.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.103.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" }
			remove_consort = yes
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = vef_queen
			set_variable = { which = queen_age value = 1100 }
		}
		hidden_effect= {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					set_country_flag = vef_a_boy
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_1_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_heir = no }
							define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT male = yes age = 0 }
							set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
							set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_2_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_3_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_4_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
					}
				}
				50 = {
					set_country_flag = vef_a_girl
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_heir = no NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_await_heir } NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_salic_law }}
							define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT female = yes age = 0 }
							set_country_flag = female_gen1_1_heir
							set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 1
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						set_country_flag = vef_twin_boy
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_1_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = { has_heir = no }
								define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT male = yes age = 0 }
								set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
								set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_2_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_3_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}

								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}

							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_4_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
						}
					}
					50 = {
						set_country_flag = vef_twin_girl
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = { has_heir = no NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_await_heir } NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_salic_law }}
								define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT female = yes age = 0 }
								set_country_flag = female_gen1_1_heir
								set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
						}

							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_heir = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }}
							NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_agnatic_senior }
						}
						AND = {
							has_female_heir = yes
							has_country_flag = vef_malepref_primo
						}
						has_heir = "Cadet Branch"
					}
				}
				determine_preemption = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = vef_a_boy
			NOT = { has_country_Flag = vef_twin_boy }
			NOT = { has_country_Flag = vef_twin_girl }
		}
		name = "vef_dynasty.104.opta"
		clr_country_flag = vef_a_boy
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = vef_a_girl
			NOT = { has_country_Flag = vef_twin_boy }
			NOT = { has_country_Flag = vef_twin_girl }
		}

			has_country_flag = vef_a_boy

					has_country_flag = vef_twin_girl
				}
				AND = {

		clr_country_flag = vef_twin_boy
		clr_country_flag = vef_twin_girl

# Healthy Birth
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.104
	title = "vef_dynasty.104.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.104.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = vef_pregnancy
		clr_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1
		clr_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2
		clr_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3
		hidden_effect= {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					set_country_flag = vef_a_boy
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_1_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_heir = no }
							define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT male = yes age = 0 }
							set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
							set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }

								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
							if = {

								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}

# Queen Dies Naturally
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.105
	title = "vef_dynasty.105.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.105.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" }
			remove_consort = yes
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = queen_age value = 1100 }}}
	}

					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f3_age which = female_gen2_4f3_age }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f3_sons which = female_gen2_4f3_sons }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f3_daughters which = female_gen2_4f3_daughters }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f4_age which = female_gen2_4f4_age }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f4_sons which = female_gen2_4f4_sons }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f4_daughters which = female_gen2_4f4_daughters }
				#END TRANSFER
				set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1100 }
				#TRANSFER KIDS#
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_daughters value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f2_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f2_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f2_daughters value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f3_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f3_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f3_daughters value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f4_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f4_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f4_daughters value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_daughters value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f2_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f2_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f2_daughters which = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f3_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f3_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f3_daughters value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f4_age value = 1100 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f4_sons value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f4_daughters value = 0 }
				#END TRANSFER
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = female_gen1_3_heir }
				kill_heir = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = fheir_3_dies
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = fheir_4_dies }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1100 }
			clr_country_flag = female_gen1_4_stored
			clr_country_flag = female_gen1_4_pregnancy
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = female_gen1_4_heir }
				kill_heir = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = fheir_4_dies
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.106.opta"
	}
}

# Death in Childbirth - Child Dies
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.107
	title = "vef_dynasty.107.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.107.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" }
			remove_consort = yes
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = vef_queen
			set_variable = { which = queen_age value = 1100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.107.opta"
	}
}

# Ruler Miscarriage
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.109
	title = "vef_dynasty.109.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.109.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = vef_pregnancy
		set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2 }
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1 }
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3 }}
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.109.opta"
	}
}

# Ruler dies in Childbirth - Child Survives
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.110
	title = "vef_dynasty.110.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.110.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect= {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					set_country_flag = vef_a_boy
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_1_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_heir = no }
							define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT male = yes age = 0 }
							set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
							set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_2_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_3_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_4_pregnancy }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
					}
				}
				50 = {
					set_country_flag = vef_a_girl
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_heir = no NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_await_heir } NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_salic_law }}
							define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT female = yes age = 0 }
							set_country_flag = female_gen1_1_heir
							set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
							check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
						}
						set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 1
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						set_country_flag = vef_twin_boy
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_1_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = { has_heir = no }
								define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT male = yes age = 0 }
								set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
								set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_2_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_3_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = male_gen1_4_pregnancy }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4m1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
						}
					}
					50 = {
						set_country_flag = vef_twin_girl
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_1f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age value = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = { has_heir = no NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_await_heir } NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_salic_law }}
								define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT female = yes age = 0 }
								set_country_flag = female_gen1_1_heir
								set_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_2f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_3f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age value = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1080 }
								check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
								check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_age value = 1080 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_sons value = 1 }}
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_gen2_4f1_daughtes value = 1 }}
							}
							set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age value = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_heir = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }}
							NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_agnatic_senior }
						}
						AND = {
							has_female_heir = yes
							has_country_flag = vef_malepref_primo
						}
						has_heir = "Cadet Branch"
					}
				}
				determine_preemption = yes
			}
		}
		kill_ruler = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.110.opta"
	}
}

# Heir Dies
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.112
	title = "vef_dynasty.112.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.112.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		government = monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		NOT = { has_reform = iqta }
		NOT = { has_reform = mamluk_government }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = male_gen0_1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen0_2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen0_3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen0_4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2m1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2m2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2m3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2m4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3m1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3m2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3m3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3m4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4m1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4m2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4m3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4m4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_1f1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_1f2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_1f3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_1f4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2f1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2f2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2f3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_2f4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3f1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3f2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3f3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_3f4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4f1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4f2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4f3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen1_4f4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen2_1m1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen2_1m2_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen2_1m3_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen2_1m4_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen2_2m1_heir
		clr_country_flag = male_gen2_2m2_heir

# New Monarch
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.113
	title = "vef_dynasty.113.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.113.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #on_actions/on_new_monarch
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		NOT = { has_reform = iqta }
		NOT = { has_reform = mamluk_government }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.113.opta"
		if = {

					has_country_flag = male_gen2_4m1_heir
				}
			}
			set_variable = { which = male_gen0_1_age value = 1100 }

			set_variable = { which = male_gen0_1_daughters value = 0 }

			clr_country_flag = male_gen1_1m1_heir

			clr_country_flag = male_gen2_3m2_heir
			clr_country_flag = male_gen2_4m2_heir

# Queen With Child
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.114
	title = "vef_dynasty.114.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.114.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = vef_pregnancy_known
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.114.opta"
	}
}

# Miscarriage
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.115
	title = "vef_dynasty.115.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.115.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = vef_pregnancy
		set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2 }
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1 }
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3 }}
			set_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.115.opta"
	}
}


####################
# NEED FOR AN HEIR #
####################
# Married With No Children; Getting Old
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.200
	title = "vef_dynasty.200.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.200.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
		government = monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		NOT = { has_reform = iqta }
		NOT = { has_reform = mamluk_government }
		is_female = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = vef_pregnancy }
		has_consort = yes
		has_foreign_consort = no
		ruler_consort_marriage_length = 5 # At least five years
		OR = {
			has_heir = no
			has_heir = "Cadet Branch"
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = vef_malepref_primo
				has_female_heir = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			ruler_age = 40
			consort_age = 30
			has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_2
		}
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { has_ruler_flag = dynasty_200_decided }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 60
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			has_heir = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			consort_age = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			ruler_age = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			has_country_flag = vef_miscarriage_3
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_ruler_flag = dynasty_200_decided }	
	
	option = { # Send Her To Convent
		trigger = { OR = { religion = catholic religion = orthodox religion = nestorian religion = coptic }}
		name = "vef_dynasty.200.opta"
		remove_consort = yes
		clr_ruler_flag = dynasty_200_decided
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_illeg_1_age value = 1080 }}
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_illeg_1_age value = 1080 }}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = dynasty_201_decided
			country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.201 days = 14 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Divorce Her
		trigger = { OR = { religion_group = muslim religion = protestant religion = reformed religion = anglican religion = presbyterian religion = anabaptist }}
		name = "vef_dynasty.200.optb"
		remove_consort = yes
		clr_ruler_flag = dynasty_200_decided
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_illeg_1_age value = 1080 }}
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = female_illeg_1_age value = 1080 }}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.201 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Name Illegitimate Son Heir
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_illeg_1_age value = 1080 }}}
		name = "vef_dynasty.200.optc"
		custom_tooltip = tt_heir_consort_conflict
		if = {
			limit = { has_female_heir = yes }
			custom_tooltip = tt_heirs_conflict
		}
		hidden_effect {
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age which = male_illeg_1_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_illeg_1_age which = male_illeg_2_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_illeg_2_age which = male_illeg_3_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_illeg_3_age which = male_illeg_4_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_illeg_4_age value = 1100 }
			set_variable = { which = heir_temp_age_calc which = male_gen1_1_age }
			set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
			set_heir_flag = vef_illegitimate
			define_male_heir = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I have a brother
		trigger = { has_female_heir = no OR = { has_country_flag = male_gen0_1_heir has_country_flag = male_gen0_2_heir has_country_flag = male_gen0_3_heir has_country_flag = male_gen0_4_heir }}
		name = "vef_dynasty.200.optd"
	}
	
	option = { # A daughter inheriting is no concern
		trigger = { has_female_heir = yes }
		name = "vef_dynasty.200.opte"
	}
	
	option = { # Do Nothing
		trigger = { has_heir = no }
		name = "vef_dynasty.200.optf"
	}
}

# Not Married; No Children but has illegitimate
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.201
	title = "vef_dynasty.201.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.201.d"
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
		government = monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		NOT = { has_reform = iqta }
		NOT = { has_reform = mamluk_government }
		has_consort = no
		is_female = no
		OR = {
			has_heir = no
			has_heir = "Cadet Branch"
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = vef_heir_gen value = 1 }}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = vef_malepref_primo
				has_female_heir = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_illeg_1_age value = 1080 }}
		NOT = { has_ruler_flag = dynasty_201_decided }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 36
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			NOT = { ruler_age = 40 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			ruler_age = 50
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_ruler_flag = dynasty_201_decided }
	
	option = { # Marry Her
		name = "vef_dynasty.201.opta"
		clr_ruler_flag = dynasty_201_decided
		define_consort = {}
		set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age which = male_illeg_1_age }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age which = male_illeg_2_age }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age which = male_illeg_3_age }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age which = male_illeg_4_age }
		set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age which = female_illeg_1_age }
		set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age which = female_illeg_2_age }
		set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age which = female_illeg_3_age }
		set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age which = female_illeg_4_age }
		set_variable = { which = male_illeg_1_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_illeg_2_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_illeg_3_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_illeg_4_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = female_illeg_1_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = female_illeg_2_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = female_illeg_3_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = female_illeg_4_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = heir_temp_age_calc which = male_gen1_1_age }
		set_country_flag = male_gen1_1_heir
		define_male_heir = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Trust in daughter
		trigger = { has_female_heir = yes }
		name = "vef_dynasty.201.optb"
	}
	
	option = { # Do Nohting
		trigger = { has_heir = no }
		name = "vef_dynasty.201.optc"
	}
}

		}
		
	}

# Fear and Loathing sequence - adapted from event 9481 in Dynasty.txt

# Part 1
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20004
	title = "vef_dynasty.20004.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20004.d"

	picture = VEF_NEW_HEIR_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		has_heir = yes
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = murdering_bastard }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = contained_insanity }
		NOT = { stability = 3 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 3600 
		modifier = { 
			factor = 3.0
			stability = 1 
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { stability = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { stability = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			NOT = { stability = -2 }
		}
	}

	# Kill the little brat
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20004.opta"
		vef_kill_heir = yes
		set_country_flag = murdering_bastard
	}

	# Maybe Prayer will work?
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = sinner_personality }
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = drunkard_personality }
		}
		name= "vef_dynasty.20004.optb"
		set_country_flag = contained_insanity
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" } }
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = "ruler_trait_pious" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
				NOT = { ruler_has_personality = pious_personality }
			}
			add_ruler_personality = pious_personality
		}
	}
	
	# I just need to get drunk to forget...
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = pious_personality }
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = entrepreneur_personality }
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = zealot_personality }
		}
		name= "vef_dynasty.20004.optc"
		add_prestige = -30
		add_legitimacy = -30
		add_horde_unity = -30
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" } }
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = "ruler_trait_drunkard" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
				NOT = { ruler_has_personality = drunkard_personality }
			}
			add_ruler_personality = drunkard_personality
		}
		set_country_flag = drunkard_ruler
	}
}

# Part 2
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20005
	title = "vef_dynasty.20005.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20005.d"

	picture = VEF_DEATH_OF_HEIR_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = murdering_bastard
		NOT = { has_country_flag = contained_insanity }
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		is_lesser_in_union = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 24 }

	# Suicide is the answer
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20005.opta"
		clr_country_flag = murdering_bastard
		kill_ruler = yes
	}

	# He's completely mad!
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20005.optb"
		add_prestige = -20
		add_legitimacy = -20
		add_horde_unity = -20
		add_years_of_income = -0.50
		add_ruler_modifier = { name = "ruler_trait_insane" }
		set_country_flag = contained_insanity
	}
}

# Part 3
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20006
	title = "vef_dynasty.20006.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20006.d"

	picture = VEF_DEATH_OF_HEIR_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = contained_insanity
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		is_lesser_in_union = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 240 }

	# Completely nuts!
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20006.opta"
		trigger = { has_heir = no }
		every_owned_province = { add_unrest = 4 }
		change_variable = { which = national_stability value = -200 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.50
		add_prestige = -20
		clr_country_flag = contained_insanity
	}

	# Abidcate = end of the chain
	option = {
		trigger = { has_heir = yes }
		name= "vef_dynasty.20006.optb"
		custom_tooltip = "insane_king_abdicates"
		hidden_effect = { kill_ruler = yes }
		add_country_modifier = { name = "relief_from" duration = 3650 }
		clr_country_flag = contained_insanity
		clr_country_flag = murdering_bastard
		clr_country_flag = drunkard_ruler
	}

	# Drunkard
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20006.optc"
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = drunkard_ruler } }
		every_owned_province = { add_unrest = 1 }
		change_variable = { which = national_stability value = -100 }
		add_prestige = -20
		add_legitimacy = -20
		add_horde_unity = -20
		add_ruler_modifier = { name= "ruler_trait_drunkard" }
	}
}

# Part 4 - Cleanup
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20007
	title = "vef_dynasty.20007.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20007.d"

	picture = VEF_DEATH_OF_HEIR_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = contained_insanity
			has_country_flag = drunkard_ruler
			has_country_flag = murdering_bastard
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = contained_insanity
		clr_country_flag = drunkard_ruler
		clr_country_flag = murdering_bastard
	}

	# Cleanup
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20007.opta"
		add_country_modifier = { name = "relief_from" duration = 3650 }
	}
}

# No heir, sequence of events - based on 'Wedding Bells' sequence in Dynastic.txt
# No Royal Marriages

# Part 1 - Setup
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20008
	title = "vef_dynasty.20008.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20008.d"

	picture = VEF_GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		prestige = 25
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { has_reform = ottoman_government }
		has_heir = no
		OR = {
			NOT = { num_of_royal_marriages = 2 }
			AND = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
				has_consort = no
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		is_at_war = no
		is_female = no
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		any_known_country = {
			religion = ROOT
			government = monarchy
			is_lesser_in_union = no
			alliance_with = ROOT
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 400 }

	# Marry
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20008.opta"
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				religion = ROOT
				government = monarchy
				is_lesser_in_union = no
				alliance_with = ROOT
				ai = yes
			}
		}
		add_legitimacy = 5
		add_horde_unity = 5
		add_prestige = 5
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = ROOT
				government = monarchy
				is_lesser_in_union = no
				alliance_with = ROOT
				ai = yes
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
					}
					define_consort = {
						country_of_origin = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			create_marriage = ROOT
		}
	}

	# No
	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20008.optb"
		add_ruler_modifier = { name = "sought_after_bachelor" }
	}
}

# Part 2 - An offer....
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20009
	title = "vef_dynasty.20009.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20009.d"

	picture = VEF_DIPLOMACY_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		any_known_country = {
			has_country_modifier = sought_after_bachelor 
			is_lesser_in_union = no
			government = monarchy
			religion_group = ROOT
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 240 }

	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20009.opta"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = sought_after_bachelor
				is_lesser_in_union = no
				government = monarchy
				religion_group = ROOT
			}
			random_list = {
				20 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.20010 }}
				80 = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.20011 }}
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -25
		add_dip_power = -25
	}

	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20009.optb"
		add_treasury = 25
		add_dip_power = 25
	}
}

# Part 3a - Marriage
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20010
	title = "vef_dynasty.20010.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20010.d"

	picture = VEF_GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20010.opta"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
			}
			define_consort = {
				country_of_origin = FROM
			}
		}
		create_marriage = FROM
		add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_marriage_offer }
		remove_country_modifier = sought_after_bachelor
		if = {
			limit = { has_heir = no }
			random = {
				chance = 25
				define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT claim = 50 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20010.optb"
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_witchcraft }
	}
}

# Part 3b - Marriage
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20011
	title = "vef_dynasty.20011.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20011.d"

	picture = VEF_GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20011.opta"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
			}
			define_consort = {
				country_of_origin = FROM
			}
		}
		create_marriage = FROM
		add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_united_dynasties }
		remove_country_modifier = sought_after_bachelor
		if = {
			limit = { has_heir = no }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT claim = 60 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name= "vef_dynasty.20011.optb"
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_refused_marriage }
	}
}

# A failed war....and unrest in the country
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20012
	title = "vef_dynasty.20012.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20012.d"

	picture = VEF_MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { government = elective_monarchy }
		has_heir = yes
		is_heir_leader = yes
		any_known_country = { truce_with = ROOT }
		is_at_war = no
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		war_exhaustion = 20
		NOT = { stability = 1 }
		heir_age = 21
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1200 }
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20012.opta"
		kill_ruler = yes
		add_war_exhaustion = -5
		every_owned_province = { add_unrest = -2 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20012.optb"
		vef_kill_heir = yes
		add_war_exhaustion = -2
		add_country_modifier = { name = "civil_turmoil" duration = 365 }
	}
}

# Heir is of our Dynasty - reworked event 9470 from Dynastic.txt
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20014
	title = "vef_dynasty.20014.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20014.d"
	picture = VEF_NEW_HEIR_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		religion_group = christian
		government = monarchy
		capital_scope = { continent = europe }
		NOT = { government = elective_monarchy }
		NOT = { government = ottoman_government }
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		num_of_royal_marriages = 3
		any_country = {
			religion_group = christian
			government = monarchy
			NOT = { government = elective_monarchy }
			NOT = { government = ottoman_government }
			marriage_with = ROOT
			NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
			has_heir = no
			is_lesser_in_union = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1500 }
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20014.opta"
		trigger = { NOT = { dynasty = "von Habsburg" } }
		add_prestige = 20
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				government = monarchy
				NOT = { government = elective_monarchy }
				NOT = { government = ottoman_government }
				marriage_with = ROOT
				NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
				has_heir = no
				is_lesser_in_union = no
			}
			define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT claim = 60 }
			add_legitimacy = 5
			add_horde_unity = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20014.optb"
		trigger = { dynasty = "von Habsburg" }
		add_prestige = 20
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				government = monarchy
				NOT = { government = elective_monarchy }
				NOT = { government = ottoman_government }
				marriage_with = ROOT
				NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
				has_heir = no
				is_lesser_in_union = no
			}
			define_heir = { dynasty = ROOT }
		}
	}
}

# The Family - event sequence reworked from event 9463 in Dynastic.txt

# Part 1 - Meanwhile in another country...
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20018
	title = "vef_dynasty.20018.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20018.d"

	picture = VEF_GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		stability = 2
		treasury = 100
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		any_known_country = {
			dynasty = ROOT
			government = monarchy
			NOT = { stability = -2 }
			NOT = { senior_union_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { junior_union_with = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 18 }
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20018.opta"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				dynasty = ROOT
				government = monarchy
				NOT = { stability = -2 }
				NOT = { senior_union_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { junior_union_with = ROOT }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = vef_dynasty.20019 days = 8 } }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dynastic_helper }
		}
		add_treasury = -100
		add_prestige = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20018.optb"
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				dynasty = ROOT
				government = monarchy
				NOT = { stability = -2 }
				NOT = { senior_union_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { junior_union_with = ROOT }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event  = { id = vef_dynasty.20020 days = 9} }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_ignore_dynasty }
		}
	}
}

# The Family Option 1
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20019
	title = "vef_dynasty.20019.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20019.d"
	picture = VEF_DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# NOTE - This add_stability should stay
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20019.opta"
		add_treasury = 100
		if = {
			limit = { stability = 3 }
			add_national_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { stability = 3 } }
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_stability = 1 }
				10 = { add_stability = 2 }
				10 = { add_stability = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Family Option 2
country_event = {
	id = vef_dynasty.20020
	title = "vef_dynasty.20020.t"
	desc = "vef_dynasty.20020.d"
	picture = VEF_DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# NOTE - This add_stability should stay
	option = {
		name = "vef_dynasty.20020.opta"
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_stability_or_adm_power = yes }
			10 = { kill_ruler = yes }
			10 = { add_stability = -2 }
		}
	}
